> <span key="e899a6d747814d328307aa26fd576751"><span offset-key="e899a6d747814d328307aa26fd576751:0">Sortable List</span></span>

> <span key="82017fa9e42840a8a8f169150d231f3b">*Let the user define an order on a list*</span>

> <span key="b0fa3ca1ac27430d8c7ebd097ba06fb8"><span offset-key="b0fa3ca1ac27430d8c7ebd097ba06fb8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/RubaXa/Sortable" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="82616e328e864c75b4c961e77f29418c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-47918_259-47919-237__"><span data-key="40116e566f3d429491213bdce53dbeef"><span data-offset-key="40116e566f3d429491213bdce53dbeef:0">sortablejs</span></span></span></a><span key="736f2025a3824371a4a8f4e7542a6a16"><span offset-key="736f2025a3824371a4a8f4e7542a6a16:0"> — Sortable — is a JavaScript library for reorderable drag-and-drop lists on modern browsers and touch devices.
